Video Rating: None
Video Description: History is replete with examples of leaders, nations, and empires who left a trail of blood behind them. But with the Bolshevik takeover of Russia after the First World War, something new crawled from the depths of the earth onto the surface of the world. Never before had a government shown such uninhibited savagery toward its own people, during peacetime, as a matter of policy and in the name of scientific management. After Nazi Germany was defeated in the Second World War, Stalin’s Soviet Union unleashed hell on the devastated nations of Eastern Europe, leaving behind an unmatched record of sadism and brutality.

*  on the eve of the Holodomor. That winter the teams operating in villages all across Ukraine [[01:22:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=4968.12s)]
*  began to search not just for grain, but for anything and everything edible. They were [[01:22:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=4974.44s)]
*  specifically equipped to do so as special tools, long metal rods, sometimes topped by [[01:22:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=4979.0s)]
*  hooks that could be used to prod any surface in search of grain. Thousands of witnesses [[01:23:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=4983.679999999999s)]
*  have described how they were used to search ovens, beds, cradles, walls, trunks, chimneys, [[01:23:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=4988.98s)]
*  attics, roofs, and cellars. To pry behind icons, into barrels, in hollow tree trunks, [[01:23:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=4994.88s)]
*  and dog houses, down wells and beneath piles of garbage. The men and women who used them [[01:23:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5000.28s)]
*  stopped at nothing, even trawling through cemeteries, barns, empty houses, and orchards. [[01:23:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5005.599999999999s)]
*  Like requisitioners of the past, they were looking for grain, but in addition they also [[01:23:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5011.3s)]
*  took fruit from trees, seeds and vegetables from kitchen gardens, as well as honey from [[01:23:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5015.5599999999995s)]
*  beehives, butter and milk, meat and sausage. Oha, Sembalyuk! Remembered that brigades took [[01:23:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5020.84s)]
*  flour, cereals, everything stored in pots, clothes, cattle. It was impossible to hide. [[01:23:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5028.64s)]
*  They searched with metal rods. They searched in stoves, broke the floors and tore away [[01:23:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5034.92s)]
*  the walls. Anastasia Pavlenko recalled that they took a bead necklace from her mother's [[01:23:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5039.32s)]
*  neck, assuming it contained something edible. Larisa Shevchuk saw party activists take away [[01:24:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5044.72s)]
*  beet and poppy seedlings that her grandmother was cultivating to plant in her vegetable [[01:24:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5050.28s)]
*  garden. Maria Bendrick from Cherkasy province wrote that the activists came and took everything. [[01:24:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5054.04s)]
*  They looked in kitchen storage tins, took away one person's kidney beans, another person's [[01:24:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5061.28s)]
*  dried crusts. They shook them out and took them away. In Kirovharad province, Leonid [[01:24:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5065.78s)]
*  Vernadub saw the brigade take down three corn cobs that had been hanging from the ceiling [[01:24:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5071.5199999999995s)]
*  to dry in preparation for use as seeds the following year. They even went around killing [[01:24:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5075.48s)]
*  the dogs and the cats in anticipation of their future use as food during the manufactured [[01:24:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5082.48s)]
*  famine. Applebaum continues, The activists also had instructions to return, to surprise [[01:24:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5088.36s)]
*  people in order to catch them unaware and with their food unguarded. Families were searched [[01:24:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5095.919999999999s)]
*  and then searched again to make sure that nothing remained. They came three times, one [[01:25:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5100.759999999999s)]
*  woman remembered, until there was nothing left, and then they stopped coming. Brigades [[01:25:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5105.4s)]
*  sometimes arrived at different times of day or night, determined to catch whoever had [[01:25:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5110.18s)]
*  food red-handed. If it happened that the family was eating a meager dinner, the activists [[01:25:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5114.12s)]
*  took the food from the table. If it happened that a soup was cooking, they pulled it off [[01:25:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5119.22s)]
*  the stove and tossed out the contents. Then they demanded to know how it was possible [[01:25:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5123.4800000000005s)]
*  that the family still had something to put in the soup. [[01:25:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5128.14s)]
*  One survivor remembered, I would go to the church up the hill and tear the bark off the [[01:25:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5133.38s)]
*  linden tree. At home we had buckwheat husks. My mother would sift them, add ground up linden [[01:25:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5137.8s)]
*  leaves and bark and bake biscuits. And that's how we ate. [[01:25:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5143.66s)]
*  And another, as the gooseberries got bigger we picked them, even though they weren't [[01:25:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5147.320000000001s)]
*  ripe. We ate wild geraniums, the acacia tree bloomed, we shook the blossoms off and ate [[01:25:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5152.12s)]
*  them. Another said, we grazed on grass and pigweed, like cattle. Any peasants who were [[01:25:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5157.84s)]
*  caught with food, or who could not meet the requisition quotas, which none of them could, [[01:26:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5165.84s)]
*  were assessed fines that none of them could pay. And then their meager belongings, whatever [[01:26:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5172.32s)]
*  furniture or clothing or farm equipment, anything that they had, would be taken away from them [[01:26:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5178.52s)]
*  to pay off the fine. The secret police and party activists would use their power over [[01:26:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5183.2s)]
*  the people for personal exploitation as well. Mothers with starving children would be forced [[01:26:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5190.88s)]
*  to prostitute themselves and their daughters to party officials in exchange for a little [[01:26:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5197.08s)]
*  bit of bread. [[01:26:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5200.84s)]
*  One woman remembered what happened to her mother. During the search, the activist asked [[01:26:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5204.32s)]
*  where was our gold and our grain? Mother replied that she had neither. She was tortured. Her [[01:26:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5209.28s)]
*  fingers were put in a door, and the door was closed. Her fingers broke, blood ran, [[01:26:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5215.36s)]
*  she lost consciousness. Water was poured over her head, and she was tortured again. They [[01:27:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5220.799999999999s)]
*  beat her and put needles under her fingernails. [[01:27:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5226.2s)]
*  Applebaum quotes two sisters. [[01:27:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5230.839999999999s)]
*  Our father hid three buckets of barley in the attic, and our mother stealthily made [[01:27:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5233.599999999999s)]
*  porridge in the evening to keep us alive. Then somebody must have denounced us, because [[01:27:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5237.44s)]
*  they took everything and brutally beat our father for not giving up the barley during [[01:27:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5242.36s)]
*  the searches. They held his fingers and slammed the door to break them. They swore at him [[01:27:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5245.839999999999s)]
*  and kicked him on the floor. It left us numb to see him beaten and sworn at like that. [[01:27:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5250.719999999999s)]
*  We were a proper family and always spoke quietly in our father's presence. [[01:27:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5257.08s)]
*  Applebaum continues. [[01:27:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5262.599999999999s)]
*  As the weeks dragged on, just being alive attracted suspicion. If a family was alive, [[01:27:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5265.36s)]
*  that meant it had food. But if they had food, then they should have given it up. And if [[01:27:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5271.58s)]
*  they had failed to give it up, then they were criminals, kulaks, Polish agents, enemies. [[01:27:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5276.14s)]
*  A brigade searching the home of Mikhailo Bolanovsky in Cherkasy province demanded to know how [[01:28:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5283.38s)]
*  it is possible that no one in this family has died yet. A brigade searching the roof [[01:28:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5288.58s)]

*  the language ruder. Why haven't you disappeared yet? Why haven't you dropped dead yet? Why [[01:28:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5306.9400000000005s)]

*  A communist state official recorded, [[01:28:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5317.06s)]
*  When traveling, I often witnessed administrative exiles haunting the villages like shadows [[01:28:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5320.58s)]
*  in search of a piece of bread or refuse. They eat carrion, slaughter dogs and cats. The [[01:28:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5325.22s)]
*  villagers keep their houses locked. Those who get a chance to enter a house drop on [[01:28:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5331.42s)]
*  their knees in front of the owner and with tears beg for a piece of bread. I witnessed [[01:28:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5335.740000000001s)]

*  found a dead body. When we sent for a policeman and a medic to pick it up, they discovered [[01:29:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5355.82s)]
*  another body inside the barn. Both died of hunger with no violence." [[01:29:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5360.34s)]
*  Before long there were no dogs and cats left to slaughter for food. There were no birds [[01:29:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5368.58s)]
*  to catch. There were no worms to dig up, no leaves on the trees or the bushes. For months [[01:29:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5375.02s)]
*  and months, nothing at all. [[01:29:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5382.58s)]
*  A ten-year-old girl without any adults left capable of taking care of her wrote a letter [[01:29:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5387.58s)]
*  to her uncle in another part of the country. [[01:29:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5394.02s)]

*  because I will die of hunger. Take me, I am small and want to live. And here I will die, [[01:30:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5413.900000000001s)]
*  because everybody dies." [[01:30:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5419.620000000001s)]
*  And there she did die, along with her parents. [[01:30:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5422.660000000001s)]
*  Starvation was a weapon of choice, not merely because it was more convenient than shooting [[01:30:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5428.1s)]
*  millions of people. And in fact, other regions of the Soviet Union suffered due to the food [[01:30:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5437.3s)]
*  shortages that occurred because of what was going on. But as with Soviet campaigns of [[01:30:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5442.660000000001s)]
*  mass terror and communal torture in other countries, the Holodomor was not only intended [[01:30:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5450.66s)]
*  to destroy the bodies of the hated Ukrainian peasantry, but to destroy the minds and the [[01:30:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5457.66s)]
*  spirits of the people who survived. To break the bonds of trust and love for family and [[01:31:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5464.66s)]
*  community that bind together a national culture that can sustain resistance to state communism. [[01:31:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5471.66s)]
*  This prolonged mass starvation drives people mad, drives a community mad, drives a country [[01:31:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5480.66s)]
*  mad, drives them into a state where morality falls away and where neighbors and families [[01:31:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5488.139999999999s)]
*  become so desperate that they are capable of doing terrible things to each other. Because [[01:31:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5493.22s)]
*  as Timothy Snyder wrote in his book, Bloodlands, those who didn't tended not to survive, quote, [[01:31:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5501.0199999999995s)]
*  The good people died first. Those who refused to steal or prostitute themselves to party [[01:31:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5507.139999999999s)]
*  officials died. Those who gave food to others died. Those who refused to eat corpses died. [[01:31:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5512.98s)]
*  Those who refused to kill their fellow man died. Parents who resisted cannibalism died [[01:32:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5520.66s)]
*  before their children did. Ukraine in 1933 was full of orphans and sometimes people took [[01:32:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5526.139999999999s)]
*  them in. Yet without food there was little that even the kindest of strangers could do [[01:32:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5532.58s)]
*  for such children. The boys and girls lay about on sheets and blankets, eating their [[01:32:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5536.82s)]
*  own excrement, waiting for death. An apple bomb records a story of a farmer who couldn't [[01:32:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5542.06s)]
*  bear any longer to watch his children suffer. The man lit a fire in the stove and closed [[01:32:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5550.0199999999995s)]
*  the chimney in order to kill them. The children began to suffocate and cry for help because [[01:32:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5555.74s)]
*  of the fumes. Then he strangled them with his own hands, after which he went to the [[01:32:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5560.52s)]
*  village council and confessed. The farmer said he had committed the murders because [[01:32:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5564.6s)]
*  there was nothing to eat. During a subsequent search of his home, no food was found at all. [[01:32:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5569.64s)]
*  Vigilantism became widespread. Armed guards would shoot gleaners on sight and anyone who [[01:32:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5576.080000000001s)]
*  tried to steal from a warehouse met the same fate. As the famine worsened, ordinary people [[01:33:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5581.360000000001s)]

*  for stealing a loaf of bread. Mikhola Basha's older brother was caught looking for spoiled [[01:33:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5601.06s)]

*  psychosis, depression, soon resulted from hunger. A woman whose six children died over [[01:33:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5621.0199999999995s)]

*  everyone that the red broom had taken her family away. One survivor recalled the horrific [[01:33:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5633.38s)]

*  of exchanging it for bread. She succeeded and returned home with a whole loaf. But when [[01:34:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5648.44s)]

*  with a paper sack, which meant that, once again, there was nothing to eat. She took [[01:34:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5659.679999999999s)]
*  the knife, turned around, stuck it into her son's back and began laughing hysterically. [[01:34:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5664.44s)]
*  Her daughter saw what was happening and ran for her life. The Soviet writer Vasily Grossman [[01:34:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5670.56s)]
*  wrote, In the beginning, starvation drives a person out of the house. In its first stage [[01:34:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5677.68s)]

*  from home. And then comes a day when the starving person crawls back into his house. [[01:34:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5699.64s)]
*  The meaning of this is that famine, starvation has won and the human being cannot be saved. [[01:35:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5706.320000000001s)]
*  He lies down on his bed and stays there, not just because he has no strength but because [[01:35:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5712.72s)]
*  he has no interest in life and no longer cares about living. He lies there quietly and does [[01:35:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=5717.3s)]

*  One of the Soviets' favorite moves when involving the local populations and establishing their [[02:00:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=7224.94s)]
*  dominance over post-war Eastern Europe was to identify and select aggrieved minorities [[02:00:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=7231.5s)]
*  in each country and put them in critical positions of power in order to assure that there would [[02:00:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=7238.5s)]

*  that it was so widely regarded as the least worst option. At the beginning of the war, [[02:12:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=7970.4s)]
*  the Germans had used their minorities in other countries as an excuse for invasion. Removing [[02:12:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=7976.4s)]
*  those minorities was considered therefore the only practical way to prevent future conflicts [[02:13:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=7981.4s)]
*  from breaking out. Even those who were forced to leave their homelands often accepted flight [[02:13:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=7986.4s)]
*  as their only option. Their lives had been made so unbearable that they regarded their [[02:13:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=7991.4s)]
*  successful transfer to another country as a lucky escape. However, population transfers [[02:13:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=7995.4s)]
*  were by no means the answer to every ethnic question after the war. Some groups could [[02:13:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8001.4s)]
*  not be driven out, no matter how unpopular they were, because they did not have their [[02:13:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8006.4s)]
*  own country to go to. Gypsies, for instance, who were everywhere almost as unwelcome as [[02:13:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8009.4s)]
*  the Jews. Some countries were obliged to integrate separate communities in an effort to cover [[02:13:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8014.4s)]
*  up the internal splits that had burst open during the war. The Czechs and the Slovaks, [[02:13:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8020.4s)]
*  for example, or to a lesser degree, the Flemings and Walloons of Belgium. In the most extreme [[02:13:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8024.4s)]
*  cases, governments were forced to pretend that ethnic problems did not exist at all, [[02:13:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8030.4s)]
*  because to acknowledge them would be politically impossible. This was the case in the USSR [[02:13:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8034.4s)]
*  and Yugoslavia, where the authorities struggled to convince the population that the violence [[02:14:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8040.4s)]
*  of the war had been the result of class differences rather than ethnic ones. Yugoslavia requires [[02:14:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8044.4s)]
*  special mention, because it encompasses all of these problems and more. Since most of [[02:14:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8050.4s)]
*  the groups who had been responsible for the violence during the war were not outsiders, [[02:14:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8055.4s)]
*  they could not be expelled. Indeed, when some tried to flee the country, they were prevented [[02:14:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8060.4s)]
*  from leaving. Nor could they be separated from one another within the country. There [[02:14:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8064.4s)]
*  were suggestions at the time that this should be done. Some individuals are asking why Serbs [[02:14:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8069.4s)]
*  shouldn't have their own federal Slavonia, stated one report by the Yugoslav Intelligence [[02:14:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8074.4s)]
*  Service, or why Croats shouldn't move to Croatia and Serbs to Serbia. But the whole purpose [[02:14:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8079.4s)]
*  of reestablishing the Yugoslavian Federation was to hold these separate nations together [[02:14:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8086.4s)]
*  under a single banner. How would Marshal Tito be able to speak of brotherhood and unity, [[02:14:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8090.4s)]
*  while at the same time banishing each nationality to separate corners of the country? And how [[02:14:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8095.4s)]
*  could he allow such nationalist tendencies to thrive while he continued to preach the [[02:15:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8100.4s)]
*  internationalism of Communist party doctrine? The different ethnic groups were therefore [[02:15:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8104.4s)]
*  obliged to continue living side by side, despite the fact that each regarded the others with [[02:15:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8109.4s)]
*  undisguised hatred. As the Ustasa regime finally abandoned Zagreb on 6 May, a measure of hysteria [[02:15:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8114.4s)]
*  took hold of the civilian population. Large numbers of refugees joined the fleeing troops. [[02:15:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8124.4s)]
*  This vast crowd, numbering hundreds of thousands, trekked northwards through Slovenia toward [[02:15:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8130.4s)]
*  the Austrian border. They were determined to reach Austria before they surrendered, [[02:15:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8135.4s)]
*  and as a consequence continued to fight long after the war was over in the rest of Europe. [[02:15:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8140.4s)]
*  The battle raged on until 15 May 1945, when the first Croatian units finally arrived on [[02:15:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8145.4s)]
*  Austrian soil at Blyberg. Here they immediately attempted to hand themselves over to British [[02:15:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8151.4s)]
*  forces. But the British refused to accept their surrender. Despite the desperate campaign [[02:15:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8157.4s)]
*  that they had just fought, the Ustasas and all their hangers-on would be obliged to hand [[02:16:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8162.4s)]
*  themselves over to the Communists after all. Accusations of betrayal have also been directed [[02:16:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8167.4s)]
*  at the way that the British treated those who did manage to surrender to them. A few days before [[02:16:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8173.4s)]
*  the arrival of the Croats, a force of about 10,000 to 12,000 Slovenian home guards had reached [[02:16:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8178.4s)]
*  Austria. The British disarmed them and put them in a camp near Vikring, a small town just a few [[02:16:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8184.4s)]
*  kilometers southwest of Klagenfur, but they had no intention of keeping them. Instead, they planned [[02:16:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8189.4s)]
*  to return them to Yugoslavia at the earliest opportunity. Realizing that the Slovenes would [[02:16:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8195.4s)]
*  resist any attempt to send them back to the Communists, the British pretended that they were only [[02:16:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8200.4s)]
*  transporting them to camps in Italy. Similar deceptions were employed against Cossacks captured [[02:16:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8205.4s)]
*  in the region, whose officers were told that they were being taken to a conference when in fact they were [[02:16:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8210.4s)]
*  to be handed over to the Soviets. Such blatant dishonesty adds weight to the body of evidence [[02:16:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8214.4s)]
*  suggesting that the British knew exactly what lay in store for these prisoners. For those who were [[02:17:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8220.4s)]
*  sent back across the Austrian border or who were captured by Tito's partisans in the northernmost [[02:17:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8225.4s)]
*  parts of Slovenia, an epic and often tragic ordeal lay ahead. A large proportion were marched along [[02:17:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8230.4s)]
*  the Drava River toward Maribor, where Tito's forces had set up transit camps. At first, these [[02:17:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8236.4s)]
*  marches were conducted in a fairly orderly manner, but they became more dangerous the further away [[02:17:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8243.4s)]
*  they progressed from the safety of Allied lines. The prisoners were given neither food nor water by [[02:17:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8248.4s)]
*  their guards, and were stripped of any valuable items such as pens, watches, wedding rings, boots, [[02:17:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8253.4s)]
*  and shoes. When gaps in the column inevitably opened up, those at the rear were ordered to run and to [[02:17:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8258.4s)]
*  catch up. To encourage them to move faster, those who lagged behind were often shot without warning. [[02:17:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8264.4s)]
*  In the 1960s, scores of testimonies were gathered from those who had experienced the forced marches [[02:17:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8269.4s)]
*  in the Yugoslavian territory, most of which agree on these details. The testimonies of German soldiers [[02:17:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8275.4s)]
*  gathered by a German government commission in the 1960s provide further corroboration. Conditions on [[02:18:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8281.4s)]
*  these death marches were extreme. As they trudged toward Maribor, Croatian soldiers and civilians [[02:18:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8287.4s)]
*  alike were gunned down using any conceivable excuse. Those who tried to escape were, of course, considered [[02:18:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8293.4s)]
*  fair game, but even stepping out of the column to relieve oneself could prove fatal. In villages along the [[02:18:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8299.4s)]
*  way, some people had left food and water for them, but anyone who made a move to gather them might also [[02:18:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8304.4s)]
*  receive a bullet. Running out of energy was not an option. One survivor, a man named Stankovic, tells the [[02:18:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8310.4s)]
*  story of a 50-year-old priest who was killed for no better reason than that he was too tired to walk any [[02:18:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8316.4s)]
*  further. Sometimes people seemed to be singled out at random. A communist officer would yell out [[02:18:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8321.4s)]
*  suddenly, kill that fellow whose head is sticking out above all the rest of the criminals. Then another [[02:18:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8327.4s)]
*  would cry, kill that little runt over there. Someone else would order that anyone wearing a beard or someone [[02:18:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8332.4s)]
*  who had been stripped of his shirt should be done away with. According to another eyewitness, the Reds [[02:18:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8338.4s)]
*  began to shoot whomever they happened to feel like shooting. In the beginning they took individuals out of the [[02:19:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8344.4s)]
*  formation and killed them in the nearby woods. Later they fired directly into the prisoner column. The shooting was [[02:19:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8349.4s)]
*  entirely indiscriminate. Many survivors speak of small groups of men being led away into the forest and shot. [[02:19:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8355.4s)]
*  One of the few contemporary accounts by a communist partisan officer tells how his comrades chose 54 [[02:19:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8361.4s)]
*  officers from amongst their prisoners to be taken out into the woods and murdered. To verify what had happened [[02:19:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8367.4s)]
*  I went up and found 54 bodies which some other soldiers were then burying. I saw pools of blood and one corpse [[02:19:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8372.4s)]
*  that had been knifed, but I reckon that the rest had been knifed also, for I only heard two or three revolver [[02:19:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8379.4s)]
*  shots and there were 54 dead. A prisoner named Franjo Krakos tells how Ustasa soldiers were singled out for [[02:19:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8384.4s)]
*  special treatment. He himself was misidentified as an Ustasa leader and immediately led off into the forest with a [[02:19:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8391.4s)]
*  group of other similar men to be shot. He escaped when one of the others ran at the guards to distract them. [[02:19:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8397.4s)]
*  Krakos' story is interesting because he escaped from partisan hands not once, but four times. Each time he was [[02:20:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8403.4s)]
*  obliged by hunger to give himself up once more. In the first instance he put his brush with death down to the [[02:20:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8410.4s)]
*  sheer bad luck of falling into the hands of a particularly sadistic group of soldiers. It was not until he was [[02:20:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8416.4s)]
*  almost executed a second time that he realized that wholesale killing was part of a wider partisan policy. [[02:20:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8422.4s)]
*  On this occasion he had his hands bound behind his back and was loaded onto one of a number of trucks along with his [[02:20:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8429.4s)]
*  fellow prisoners. After a ride of about 20 minutes we were unloaded like sacks of wheat at Maribor Island, which is [[02:20:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8435.4s)]
*  upstream from the town. As we approached this place we heard the staccato firing of a machine gun along with single [[02:20:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8442.4s)]
*  rifle shots from time to time. So we had now no doubt concerning our fate. I landed on my feet when I was tossed out of [[02:20:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8448.4s)]
*  the truck. Thus I was able to take a good look at a scene of horror that would have inspired a 20th century Dante. [[02:20:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8455.4s)]
*  What absorbed my interest were several mass graves which had been dug about 300 yards apart. Since they were almost [[02:21:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8462.4s)]
*  filled with bodies I could not determine how deep they were. I judged that each of them contained perhaps 300 corpses. On top of [[02:21:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8468.4s)]
*  these masses of cadavers I could discern movement. Some of the victims were still alive. Out of these grisly holes came [[02:21:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8476.4s)]
*  screams, Brother, kill me, shoot me once more. I remember that cry being repeated several times. Also there were [[02:21:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8483.4s)]
*  unwounded men in the graves who were smothering as bodies were thrown on top of them. They were trying to make themselves [[02:21:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8491.4s)]
*  heard too. Some intended victims were trying to get away into the woods and the partisans were shooting at them. Trucks drove [[02:21:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8497.4s)]
*  up bringing other groups of prisoners. As the guards started to unload them the volume of rifle and machine gun fire [[02:21:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8503.4s)]
*  increased tremendously because the prisoners made a break for it as soon as they hit the ground. Although my hands were still [[02:21:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8509.4s)]
*  bound behind my back I also took off at a run. Bullets were whacking into the trees and cutting the shrubbery all around me. I tripped [[02:21:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8515.4s)]
*  over a fallen branch and fell down headlong. Probably this saved me because the guards evidently thought that I was accounted for [[02:22:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8522.4s)]
*  and turned their attention elsewhere. It is obvious from accounts like this that far from being the actions of a few isolated [[02:22:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8528.4s)]
*  individuals the killing of Croatian prisoners by the communist partisans was the work of entire units of men. It was also fairly [[02:22:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8536.4s)]
*  well organized. Prisoners were executed not only individually and in small groups but on a massive scale. Slaughter like this would not [[02:22:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8543.4s)]
*  have been possible without an element of central organization by authorities. The local headquarters of these authorities appeared to [[02:22:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8551.4s)]
*  have been at the nearby town of Maribor. Nearer to the town were long lines of anti-tank trenches which had been dug by German troops [[02:22:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8558.4s)]
*  as a last-ditch defense against the communists. Prisoners were brought here by truckload where they were lined up along the edge of the [[02:22:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8565.4s)]
*  trench and shot. These prisoners knew precisely what lay in store for them because they could see the corpses of previous groups of [[02:22:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8571.4s)]
*  prisoners lying at the bottoms of the trenches. Many of them had been stripped of all their clothes. They had their hands bound behind [[02:22:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8578.4s)]
*  their backs to prevent them trying to escape or lash out at their guards. The following account is by a Croatian officer who, like many who [[02:23:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8585.4s)]
*  escaped Yugoslavia but still had relatives there during the Cold War, wished to remain anonymous. [[02:23:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8593.4s)]
*  In the evening the communists undressed us, tied our hands behind our backs with a wire and then tied us two-and-two. After that we were taken in trucks [[02:23:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8599.4s)]
*  to the east of Maribor. I managed to untie my hands but was still tied to the other officer. We were brought to huge ditches where there were [[02:23:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8608.4s)]
*  already dead bodies piled. The communists started shooting at our backs. Fast as lightning I threw myself on top of the dead bodies. More dead bodies [[02:23:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8616.4s)]
*  fell on top of me. When the partisans were through shooting our group they left. They did not bury us because there was room for more. So they went to [[02:23:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8625.4s)]
*  Maribor for more victims. I untied myself from my dead partner and crawled out of this mass grave. I was naked and covered with the blood of other victims [[02:23:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8633.4s)]
*  and so full of fear that I could not walk very far. I climbed a tree not far from the execution place. Three more times the communists arrived with [[02:24:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8642.4s)]
*  officers and priests and killed them all. When the sun started to rise I went away. The killing at Maribor lasted several days and when the [[02:24:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8651.4s)]
*  anti-tank trenches were full special burial squads were detailed to pile earth across them and then level them off. Bodies were also buried in shell holes, [[02:24:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8660.4s)]
*  bomb craters and specially dug mass graves. One former communist partisan who later fled Yugoslavia gave a graphic description of what it was like to work on one of these [[02:24:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8670.4s)]
*  burial parties. As we were performing our grim duty another group was detailed to dig out a large hole that began where the trenches ended. To my horror I saw that [[02:24:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8679.4s)]
*  this pit too was full of bodies. Since the dead in this hole were quite stiff or already putrefying they probably had been killed days before. We were still engaged in the [[02:24:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8689.4s)]
*  task of burial at 5pm when a hundred prisoners were brought to the newly excavated abattoir. We were told that they were going to help us inter the dead but then these [[02:24:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8699.4s)]
*  prisoners were lined up at the edge of the hole where the other corpses lay. Next they were looted of what belongings they had. And finally the hundred prisoners were machine [[02:25:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8708.4s)]
*  gunned. I watched this slaughter from a distance of 100 yards or less. Some of the prisoners threw themselves down flat and escaped the machine gun fire. They pretended to be dead [[02:25:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8717.4s)]
*  but the partisans went from one apparent corpse to another and ran their bayonets through everyone whom they suspected of being alive. Screams rent the air providing [[02:25:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8726.4s)]
*  grim evidence that those who had dodged the machine gun fire had not eluded death for long. All of the new victims were thrown into the hole on top of the old corpses. Then the [[02:25:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8736.4s)]
*  partisans directed several more bursts of machine gun fire into the pile of bodies just to make sure that they had not left anyone alive. Maribor was by no means the only place where such [[02:25:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8746.4s)]
*  massacres occurred. The vast majority of the 12,000 members of the Slovenian National Army who had escaped to Austria and who were then handed back to the communists by the British were [[02:25:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8757.4s)]
*  murdered in the forests. They were taken to the edge of deep ravines and either shot or thrown over the edge alive. The walls of the ravines were then dynamited in order to topple masses of rock [[02:26:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8766.4s)]
*  under the corpses below. According to eyewitnesses there was no discrimination between the victims. There was no questioning of the prisoners nor did any of them receive any kind of trial nor was there any [[02:26:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8777.4s)]
*  selection made among them. Everyone who was brought was doomed to die. At least 8,000 to 9,000 Slovenians were killed in this way as well as some Croatians, Montenegrin Chetniks and members of three [[02:26:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8788.4s)]
*  Serbian Volunteer Corps regiments. There were also a handful of women amongst the victims and around 200 members of the Ustasa youth movement aged between 14 and 16. Similar events occurred in an abyss at Podutic, only a few kilometers [[02:26:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8801.4s)]
*  outside Ljubljana. Here the mass of decomposing bodies began to contaminate Ljubljana's water supply so in June a group of German POWs were made to exhume the bodies and bury them in mass graves. The communists [[02:26:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8815.4s)]
*  used any and all methods in order to kill their victims. In Lascaux and Hrastnik, Croatians were thrown down mine shafts and hand grenades thrown in after them. In Rifnik, prisoners were driven into a bunker that was then blown up with them [[02:27:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8828.4s)]
*  inside it. In the POW camp at Bezograd, prisoners were locked inside an enclosed reservoir which was then flooded until they were all drowned. In Istria, on the border between Yugoslavia and Italy, hundreds of Italian prisoners were thrown down deep pits and ravines [[02:27:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8841.4s)]
*  to their deaths. Inevitably, as at Maribor, there were some who managed to survive. One survivor, who was shot along with hundreds of others at Kamnik, tells a story that, were it not for the terrifying circumstances, might seem almost comic. He and his fellow prisoners were told to form a circle, after which the guards opened fire on them. Despite being hit in the forehead, he somehow survived. As he lay amongst his dead and dying comrades, he heard the partisans arguing amongst themselves. They were all killed. [[02:27:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8856.4s)]
*  They were quite upset, because when the fools lined us up in a circle and began firing, they were spread out in a circle too, outside of ours. Thus, in effect, they were shooting one another as well as us. Two partisans were killed, and two others severely wounded because of this bit of stupidity. [[02:28:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8885.4s)]
*  End quote. [[02:28:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8901.4s)]
*  This is explaining the mass murder by Yugoslav communists after the war. Tito's deputy, Milovan Djilas, put it this way. [[02:28:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8906.4s)]
*  Yugoslavia was in a state of chaos and destruction. There was hardly any civil administration. There were no properly constituted courts. There was no way in which the cases of 20,000 to 30,000 people could have been reliably investigated. So, the easy way out was to have them all shot, and to have done with the problem. So we put an end to it, once and for all. [[02:28:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8914.4s)]
*  In many other countries, resistance to communist domination was not something that they were able to put an end to once and for all so quickly. Some places it continued for years. Ukrainian nationalists fought for many years for their country's independence. [[02:28:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8937.4s)]
*  The Baltic states, Estonia, Latvia, Lithuania, fought well into the 1950s, hoping in vain for Western support that never materialized, and they did so without the baggage of widespread ethnic cleansing that was carried out by the Ukrainian resistance. [[02:29:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8955.4s)]
*  When the Soviets swept into the Baltic states in the fall of 44, many thousands of Estonians, Latvians, and Lithuanians had already had a taste of Stalinist rule, and it had enough of it, and intended to die before submitting to it again. [[02:29:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8971.4s)]
*  And so they left their homes, they left their families, some of them living on the run for a while, moving from place to place, and then after a while, eventually most of them took up residence in the forest. [[02:29:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8987.4s)]
*  And then from the forest, they found each other, and they began to organize and launch guerrilla attacks against communist forces. [[02:29:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=8999.4s)]
*  Their lives were hungry and cold. They were scrounging for food or accepting it from courageous sympathizers who risked their lives and their families' lives merely by associating with the fugitives. [[02:30:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9009.4s)]
*  Any of them who were wounded in battle could count on little more than basic first aid, and even that with very limited supplies. It was a hard life for many years for some of these people. [[02:30:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9022.4s)]
*  Among the Baltic fighters were enough military men that they were able to organize themselves into a competent force at arms. [[02:30:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9034.4s)]
*  Men and women were organized into units with a military-style command structure, and tasks such as the building of shelters and bunkers, as well as gathering and distributing food and other supplies was handled in a fairly organized manner. [[02:30:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9041.4s)]
*  The Lithuanians were particularly fierce and numerous, often engaging not only in hit-and-run tactics, but getting into pitched battles against small Red Army contingents and ambushing NKVD soldiers, [[02:30:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9056.4s)]
*  assassinating communist leaders, and launching attacks even on prisons to free their comrades that had been taken captive. [[02:31:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9067.4s)]
*  In May 1945, as the war was coming to an end in Europe, Lithuanian militiamen engaged a large force of NKVD men in a forest in the southern part of that country. [[02:31:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9076.4s)]
*  They were led by a former army officer named Jonas Nefalta, a nationalist respected for having fought against both the Nazis and the Soviets. [[02:31:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9086.4s)]
*  Nefalta had been on the Soviet kill list since the Red Army first moved into the country in 1940, but he'd managed to evade murder while helping to lead the resistance even as conditions kept rapidly changing. [[02:31:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9096.4s)]
*  The previous summer, in 1944, Nefalta had taken a Soviet bullet to the chest, but he was able to escape the hospital where the communists had placed him under armed guard. [[02:31:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9108.4s)]
*  After he escaped, he made his way to an out-of-the-way farm that belonged to a relative, and once he'd recovered a bit, he gathered his wife and the two of them took to the forest. [[02:31:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9118.4s)]
*  Because there could be no question of leaving your loved ones out of the fight with the Soviets. [[02:32:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9127.4s)]
*  They had been infamous since the revolution for taking family members as hostages and threatening their torture and murder against the continued absence of any fugitive. [[02:32:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9132.4s)]
*  And so for six months, the two gathered up the other fugitives and refugees that they found and began to organize and train them in basic combat operations and survival skills. [[02:32:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9142.4s)]
*  And then their ragtag group began a campaign against the Soviets and their local collaborators. [[02:32:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9151.4s)]
*  Well, after a while, the communists had had enough of this group of guerrillas, and they sent a large detachment of NKVD troops into the Konigsgis forest in mid-May 1945. [[02:32:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9157.4s)]
*  NKVD got a bead on the general area where Nefalta was located with his people, and they surrounded it in a wide net and began to move in. [[02:32:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9169.4s)]
*  Seeing that there was no way out, Nefalta and his followers fell back to a hill in the middle of the forest, quickly erected some makeshift fortifications and got ready to fight. [[02:32:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9178.4s)]
*  And with small arms and a few grenades, which is all they had, they fought for hours and hours, but before long they were coming down to the last of their ammunition. [[02:33:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9191.4s)]
*  And so the only hope of avoiding a general massacre of every one of them was to somehow break through the Soviet lines. [[02:33:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9199.4s)]
*  So Nefalta took the two dozen or so of his remaining fighters, gathered up all the rest of their ammunition, and they attacked with full force a single point in the Soviet cordon. [[02:33:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9206.4s)]
*  And they broke through and they made their way to a nearby marshland and made their way to safety. [[02:33:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9216.4s)]
*  Behind them lay 44 of their dead comrades, including Nefalta's wife, who died with a machine gun in her hands. [[02:33:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9220.4s)]
*  They did not go to their deaths without company. They had killed over 400 NKVD men. [[02:33:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9228.4s)]
*  But of course, this is the Soviet military. They could lose 400 men every day for a year without being seriously degraded. [[02:33:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9235.4s)]
*  Nefalta, being a traditional army officer, was very brave and he was an inspiring leader, but his mentality was not particularly well suited to guerrilla operations. [[02:34:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9245.4s)]
*  It's a shame somebody couldn't have gotten him a copy of Mao's Manual on guerrilla warfare or something. [[02:34:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9256.4s)]
*  Losing 44 fighters to inflict 400 KIA on the enemy is a huge success in any traditional military context, but Nefalta lost half his people that day. [[02:34:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9261.4s)]
*  In that November, he and his remaining partisans were once again surrounded, this time at a farmhouse, and after a fierce firefight, Jonas Nefalta fell in battle. [[02:34:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9272.4s)]
*  But the Soviet government was becoming concerned with the determination and the ferocity of the Baltic resistance. [[02:34:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9284.4s)]
*  Lavrentiy Beria, head of the NKVD, one of the most sadistic men in the Soviet government, truly evil monster, [[02:34:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9291.4s)]
*  he sent General Sergei Kruglov to crush the Baltic rebellion. [[02:35:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9301.4s)]
*  Kruglov had just recently completed a swift and savage campaign of ethnic cleansing against the Tatars of Crimea, [[02:35:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9305.4s)]
*  loading some 200,000 of them into cattle cars over just a few days and deporting them to Kazakhstan and in the process killing at least a quarter of all Crimean Tatars, some 40,000 to 80,000 people. [[02:35:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9312.4s)]
*  And his methods were of the kind to please a man like Lavrentiy Beria. [[02:35:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9324.4s)]
*  One of the cornerstones of Soviet methods was the use of torture. [[02:35:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9331.4s)]
*  This usually took the form of beating prisoners, a practice that was so common and so violent that in one district of Latvia, 18% of police suspects were reported to have died during interrogation. [[02:35:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9335.4s)]
*  Other methods included the administering of electric shocks, burning the skin with cigarettes, slamming doors on prisoners' hands and fingers, and waterboarding. [[02:35:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9347.4s)]
*  One former prisoner suffered the same torture as the hero of George Orwell's 1984. [[02:35:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9356.4s)]
*  Eleonora Lubanaskin was locked in a toilet stall the size of a telephone booth along with 50 rats released from a cage. [[02:36:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9361.4s)]
*  Such torture was officially frowned upon by the Soviet authorities, but in reality it was sanctioned at every level of the Soviet administration. [[02:36:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9370.4s)]
*  Stalin himself had claimed before the war that the use of torture was absolutely correct and useful because it brought results and greatly accelerated the unmasking of enemies of the people. [[02:36:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9378.4s)]
*  While the torture did provide the authorities with intelligence, it also had other, less welcome results. [[02:36:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9389.4s)]
*  All partisan memoirs state with pride that the Flores brothers would rather die than surrender. [[02:36:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9396.4s)]
*  And there are numerous stories of partisan units trying to shoot their way out of hopeless situations rather than giving themselves up peacefully. [[02:36:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9402.4s)]
*  This is not mere myth. Soviet reports also describe the extraordinary determination of partisans in both Ukraine and Lithuania to die fighting. [[02:36:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9409.4s)]
*  For example, a Lithuanian police report from January 1945 describes how security troops surrounded a house containing 25 partisans who refused to surrender even after the house was set on fire. [[02:36:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9418.4s)]
*  Five of these partisans broke out and crawled across a field towards a machine gun crew in an attempt to silence it. [[02:37:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9430.4s)]
*  They were shot one by one, but did not give up advancing until they were all dead. [[02:37:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9436.4s)]
*  The rest of the group carried on fighting from the burning house until it finally collapsed and buried them. [[02:37:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9441.4s)]
*  The use of torture was just one element of a system that was designed to terrorize both the partisans and their support networks amongst the civilian population. [[02:37:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9446.4s)]
*  Other methods of intimidation included the public hanging of local guerrilla leaders, the deportation of those suspected of links to the resistance, and the display of dead bodies in market squares. [[02:37:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9456.4s)]
*  In his memoir, Giozas Luksa gives half a dozen examples of dead partisans being propped up in villages, sometimes in obscene poses, as a method of terrorizing the population. [[02:37:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9467.4s)]
*  Even his own brother's body was treated this way. [[02:37:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9479.4s)]
*  Sometimes the NKVD would force local residents to come and look at the bodies, and their reactions were observed in order to discover where their loyalties lay. [[02:38:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9482.4s)]
*  If they saw people passing by the corpses who revealed any sadness or pity, they would go out and arrest them and torture them, demanding that they reveal the names and surnames of the dead men. [[02:38:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9491.4s)]
*  There are numerous stories of parents being shown their dead children and being obliged to show no emotion for fear of betraying themselves. [[02:38:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9501.4s)]
*  The price of revealing one's loyalties in situations like this could be high. [[02:38:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9510.4s)]
*  Zealous security officials thought nothing of targeting the friends and family of known partisans if they thought it might flush the insurgents out into the open. [[02:38:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9514.4s)]
*  The very least such people could expect was arrest and interrogation followed by the threat of deportation to Siberia. [[02:38:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9522.4s)]
*  This was perhaps another reason that the partisans were so reluctant to give themselves up during a siege. [[02:38:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9529.4s)]
*  Many who found themselves surrounded would hold a grenade to their heads and blow themselves up, specifically so that the Soviets would not be able to identify them and so be able to target their families. [[02:38:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9535.4s)]
*  Sometimes Soviet security forces would resort to even more brutal methods amongst the general population. [[02:39:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9546.4s)]
*  The burning of homes and farms was widespread in Lithuania as a method of punishing suspected partisans and terrorizing their families and communities. [[02:39:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9552.4s)]
*  Eventually the practice was banned by the chief of the security troops himself, but it seems that his objections were not on the grounds that the practice was unlawful, but because he suspected that his troops were targeting innocent civilians as a way to avoid fighting the real partisans. [[02:39:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9561.4s)]
*  We have an account from one of the NKVD soldiers engaged in this campaign. [[02:39:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9578.4s)]
*  Private Janin set the house on fire from the outside. [[02:39:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9584.4s)]
*  When an old woman, crossing herself, came out of the house, followed by a girl, Lipin told them to go back into the burning house. [[02:39:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9588.4s)]
*  Then the old woman and the girl started to run. Lipin took out his pistol and began shooting at each of them, but missed. [[02:39:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9595.4s)]
*  One soldier shot down the old woman, while Lipin ran after the girl and shot her at close range. [[02:40:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9602.4s)]
*  Then he ordered two soldiers to take the bodies and throw them through the window into the house. [[02:40:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9607.4s)]
*  The soldiers took the old woman by the hands and feet and threw her into the burning house, then did the same with the corpse of the girl. [[02:40:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9612.4s)]
*  Soon an old man and the elder's son ran out of the house, through another door. Soldiers opened fire but could not get them. [[02:40:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9619.4s)]
*  Then I and two other soldiers were ordered to catch and kill the son, but we failed as it was dark and he escaped. [[02:40:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9626.4s)]
*  On returning to the house we started combing the rye field. We found the old man there. He was wounded and crawling through the rye. [[02:40:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9633.4s)]
*  One of the soldiers finished him off and we brought the corpse to the house. [[02:40:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9640.4s)]
*  For years the Lithuanians and the Estonians and the Latvians fought like heroes for their freedom from Soviet tyranny and did so against the odds of Barkhopa. [[02:40:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9647.4s)]
*  There was no hope here. [[02:41:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9660.4s)]
*  The 100,000 plus Lithuanians and the 20,000 to 40,000 each of Estonians and Latvians drew inspiration from stories like these, of these men and women who became known as the Forrest Brothers. [[02:41:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9662.4s)]
*  And that helped carry them through long years of deprivation and cold and the extreme brutality of the Soviets. [[02:41:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9677.4s)]
*  Over the years their real heroic deeds were mixed in with legend and the stories became part of the national mythology of these tiny countries. [[02:41:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9686.4s)]
*  In one of them a famous Estonian partisan named Antskaljurand, known as Ants the Terrible, was being hunted by the NKVD. [[02:41:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9694.4s)]
*  But according to the story he liked to taunt and brazenly defy them by announcing his imminent arrival into a new district by mail ahead of time. [[02:41:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9704.4s)]
*  And so the story is that Ants the Terrible was going to arrive in Parnu and so he mailed a particular restaurant manager that when he got there he expected to have a hearty meal waiting for him. [[02:41:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9713.4s)]
*  And so of course the manager passed the letter on to the authorities and NKVD men in plain clothes filled and surrounded the restaurant to win ambush. [[02:42:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9723.4s)]
*  But somehow Ants the Terrible had managed to commandeer a Russian car and the uniform of a high ranking Russian officer and the unsuspecting secret policeman just let him walk right in past them, enjoy his meal and then walk right back out. [[02:42:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9734.4s)]
*  And the way the legend goes under his plate he left a generous tip and a thank you note signed in his own name, Ants the Terrible. [[02:42:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9747.4s)]
*  And so stories like that nourish hungry fighters for a hopeless cause. [[02:42:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9756.4s)]
*  The last well-known resistance fighter was not captured until 1956 and as late as 1965 Lithuanian partisans were still being hunted down and still fighting with Soviet forces. [[02:42:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9760.4s)]
*  The last Estonian partisan was not killed until the late 70s. [[02:42:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9771.4s)]
*  And even though they lost their sacrifice was not in vain. [[02:42:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9777.4s)]
*  Even after the Soviets had consolidated power over their countries the names of the Forest Brothers remained as a subterranean rallying cry for resistance against total submission to Soviet domination. [[02:43:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9780.4s)]
*  And they re-emerged as popular heroes as the Baltics began to break away and re-establish their power. [[02:43:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9793.4s)]
*  It's a hard question that question of whether it's better to fight to the bitter end even with no real hope of victory. [[02:43:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9799.4s)]
*  To this day Jews debate whether the suicides at Masada were an example of holy dedication or amoral extremism. [[02:43:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=9808.4s)]
