*  They had to take certain measures that were similar to the ones they took in other countries. [[02:58:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10699.4s)]
*  For example, they didn't trust the army, they didn't trust the police, and so while these were still used for basic law enforcement, Communist militias were used for more important or politically sensitive tasks. [[02:58:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10704.4s)]
*  In Romania, as in other countries, the Soviets often empowered aggrieved minorities by placing them in politically significant positions. [[02:58:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10716.4s)]
*  In Romania, in the immediate post-war period, this often meant Jewish Communists, because Jews had not had an easy time in Romania during the war, or even before the war really, to say the least. [[02:58:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10727.4s)]
*  And some of those who made it through were more than happy to take up positions of power over the people that they perceived as their persecutors. [[02:58:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10739.4s)]
*  And so as a result, the head of the Communist Party in Romania, and the interior minister in charge of the military police, and the head of prisons, and the foreign minister, and the head of the secret police, for much of the time from the Communist takeover, [[02:59:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10749.4s)]
*  these positions were filled by Romanian Jewish Communists until Stalin got paranoid about Zionism in the early 50s and started purging them. [[02:59:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10763.4s)]
*  This is obviously a very difficult aspect of the story to talk about, given the way that it's used to reinforce anti-Semitic attitudes, including in many of these countries to this day. [[02:59:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10772.4s)]
*  But again, you always have to remember that even if the whole upper echelon of the government consisted of Jews, which it didn't, you're still just talking about a handful of people. [[02:59:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10783.4s)]
*  You can always find a handful of people from any group to carry out some evil for you. [[02:59:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10796.4s)]
*  If you colonized the United Kingdom and wanted to install a terror regime to unleash hell on the English population, you could probably still find enough Irish nationalists who have enough hatred for the British to fill a lot of key roles in the administration, [[03:00:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10802.4s)]
*  but that doesn't really tell us anything at all about what most Irish people feel or what they would be willing to do. [[03:00:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10818.4s)]
*  Anyway, this was a tactic by the Soviets. That's why you see it repeated in several countries and why you saw similar tactics in European colonial governments around the world. [[03:00:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10824.4s)]
*  Syria to this day is a majority Sunni Muslim country run by a Shiite Muslim government. [[03:00:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10835.4s)]
*  Until the Iraq war, Iraq was majority Shiite country run by a Sunni government. Neither of those were by accident. [[03:00:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10841.4s)]
*  In both cases, the French and the British found a group that they could put in charge that the majority of the local population would not be particularly thrilled about. [[03:00:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10848.4s)]
*  And who knew that if they lost their position, whether it was because they lost the favor of the colonial master or because they weren't willing to employ the sufficiently harsh methods to suppress popular opposition, they would be the first ones to suffer. [[03:00:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10857.4s)]
*  In each of the Eastern European countries, as you get out of the immediate post-war period and as the communist government stabilized and their power was more secure, you saw a transition away from governance by minorities to government primarily by the local ethnicity. [[03:01:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10872.4s)]
*  I think that Romania in the late 40s and early 50s provides the clearest and most unobstructed view of what Soviet communism was when they had full control and the brakes were removed. [[03:01:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10888.4s)]
*  Again, this was partly because the presence of existing institutions such as the internal security service allowed the communists to establish total control more quickly than would have otherwise been possible. [[03:01:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10910.4s)]
*  And so it allowed them to go to work on the population almost right away. [[03:02:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10923.4s)]
*  By the time they were able to achieve that in some of these other countries, the darkest period of the Stalinist era had passed and the Soviet Union had started to change a little bit. [[03:02:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10928.4s)]
*  And that work they wanted to do on the population in Romania had all the normal features, of course, you know, pervasive informants and secret police, show trials, imprisonment and murder of dissidents, and the casual use of torture. [[03:02:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10941.4s)]
*  And torture is what we're going to end the episode talking about. [[03:02:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10957.4s)]
*  Torture can be used for many purposes and for many reasons. [[03:02:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10964.4s)]
*  It can be used to terrorize and intimidate. [[03:02:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10970.4s)]
*  It can just be a matter of revenge. [[03:02:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10974.4s)]
*  And, of course, it can be used to extract information from someone who doesn't want to give it up. [[03:02:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10977.4s)]
*  Premodern societies typically employed torture as a central pillar of regime security and legal punishment. [[03:03:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10984.4s)]
*  And so torture was frequently performed in public, according to strict rituals in which both the torturer and the tortured, as well as the audience, all had their roles to play in the drama. [[03:03:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=10991.4s)]
*  Often, as the victim was being tortured on his way to execution, he would put on a bit of a performance, kind of gain the sympathy of the crowd. [[03:03:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11004.4s)]
*  Dan Carlin has a great episode about this where he kind of discusses some incidents that make it really clear the roles different people had to play. [[03:03:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11014.4s)]
*  He gained the sympathy of the crowd first by demonstrating toughness and resolve in the face of his suffering, but then by coming back into the social fold, so to speak, by repenting of his actions and begging for forgiveness. [[03:03:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11022.4s)]
*  And he also shows us the power of kindness and mercy. [[03:03:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11034.4s)]
*  We've learned a lot since then, and in a way, we might know better what they were really up to back then than they even knew themselves. [[03:03:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11038.4s)]
*  Or at least we're able to describe it with fewer metaphors and analogies. [[03:04:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11046.4s)]
*  In our day, as Foucault described, official punishment has been transferred primarily from the body to the mind or the spirit, if you like. [[03:04:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11050.4s)]
*  It's not unusual to assign someone 20 lashes, but not 20 years in a cell. [[03:04:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11059.4s)]
*  This transition from physical to psychological punishment reflects a deeper understanding of the true purpose of torture, which is made explicit when it's used to extract information from an unwilling participant. [[03:04:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11065.4s)]
*  That is, torture of the body is just a back door. [[03:04:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11083.4s)]
*  It's an indirect route to the real target, which is the mind. [[03:04:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11087.4s)]
*  This was true even in pre-modern examples of public display, which is why the intention and goal of those displays was to bring the show to a climax with the repentance and absolution of the guilty victim. [[03:04:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11092.4s)]
*  Torture is not meant only to break down the will to resist further pain. [[03:05:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11105.4s)]
*  It's meant to reduce the victim to a pliable, almost infantile state of openness, and dependency on the torturer. [[03:05:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11111.4s)]
*  Our contemporary discussions about torture tend to center on its ineffectiveness for extracting reliable information from people. [[03:05:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11122.4s)]
*  But that unreliability is largely due to the fact that you can never really be sure whether the person you're torturing actually knows anything at all. [[03:05:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11129.4s)]
*  If you get a pool of people and you torture them for information, unless you mess up and accidentally kill them, or unless they're one of those monks during the Vietnam War and can just go into some trance while you're doing whatever it is you're going to do, they're all going to break and tell you something eventually. [[03:05:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11138.4s)]
*  Especially if they know that you can wait. [[03:05:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11158.4s)]
*  But for all you know, none of them have any valuable information, and you were probably better off having no information at all than a flood of bad information to sift through. [[03:06:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11162.4s)]
*  But a skilled torturer, given enough time, doesn't really have to extract information from unwilling subjects. [[03:06:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11171.4s)]
*  If a torturer knows his job and has enough time, again, that is really critical, the subject will tell his persecutor what he wants to know, not simply for a reprieve from the pain, but because he wants to. [[03:06:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11182.4s)]
*  Because he wants to please his torturer. [[03:06:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11198.4s)]
*  Genuinely wants to gain his approval. [[03:06:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11201.4s)]
*  Extended torture of a fully captive individual or group drives subjects through the back wall of the psyche into such a state of dependency that they'll actually blame themselves and not their captor for every new prick of the knife or crush of the hammer. [[03:06:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11206.4s)]
*  This is why sophisticated torturers know to construct little games where the victim seems to bring the pain upon himself. [[03:07:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11226.4s)]
*  He'll be given an impossible task and then punished when it's not accomplished to the torturer's satisfaction, which is of course completely arbitrary. [[03:07:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11234.4s)]
*  He may be told to stand with his arms straight out to the sides holding a weight in each hand, and told that he'll be beaten if his arms drop. [[03:07:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11242.4s)]
*  When he drops his arms, inevitably he is beaten, and he blames himself for failing to keep his arms raised. [[03:07:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11249.4s)]
*  Even though he knows on some rational level that this is all designed for him to get another beating. [[03:07:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11258.4s)]
*  He's not going to blame himself the first time, he might not blame himself the second time or the third time, but we know quite a bit now about how the human mind works in extremis. [[03:07:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11266.4s)]
*  Soviet and American intelligence agencies were experimenting with drugs and hypnosis and sleep deprivation as a means to extract information from people. [[03:07:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11277.4s)]
*  They were attempting to remove the messy step of bodily suffering in order to go straight at the mind, to attack the mind directly. [[03:08:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11287.4s)]
*  Attempts to implant information and even take control of a subject's personality. [[03:08:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11296.4s)]
*  So we're based on the understanding that the ultimate goal of torture is the complete breakdown of the personality. [[03:08:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11301.4s)]
*  So that it could then be reordered according to principles determined by the master. [[03:08:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11309.4s)]
*  One of the stated goals of these programs was to see if they could take somebody and have them reverse their most closely held and deepest feelings. [[03:08:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11316.4s)]
*  Their deepest moral beliefs. Can we get them to violate those? Can we get them to not even believe in those? [[03:08:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11330.4s)]
*  The spiritual warfare carried on in Romanian prisons in the immediate post-war period allows us to see that incidents such as what happened at Abu Ghraib in Iraq, [[03:08:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11338.4s)]
*  where humiliation was a key technique approved by interrogators, or at the Waco siege in the 90s where threats and sleep deprivation and other means of psychological terror were employed against the people there. [[03:09:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11350.4s)]
*  That those meet the definition of torture as surely as beatings and fingernail extractions. They're just more sophisticated. [[03:09:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11363.4s)]
*  The communists were dogmatic materialists, and so they approached torture as a scientific endeavor. [[03:09:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11373.4s)]
*  It was applied behavioral psychology to them. Just as dogs could be modified into almost entirely new creatures through operant conditioning, [[03:09:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11380.4s)]
*  so could human beings be transformed into the new Marxist man by a consistent clinical application of Pavlovian reinforcement. [[03:09:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11391.4s)]
*  Later on, the Soviet Union would weaponize psychology in a very sophisticated way to pathologize all forms of dissent and dissatisfaction with the party. [[03:10:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11400.4s)]
*  In this earlier stage, the methods are cruder, but the goals are maybe more ambitious. [[03:10:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11409.4s)]
*  Viktor Frankl, the existentialist and psychologist who survived the Nazi camps and wrote a book called Man's Search for Meaning based on his reflections on those experiences, [[03:10:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11417.4s)]
*  he wrote that, everything can be taken from a man but one thing, the last of his human freedoms, to choose one's attitude in any given set of circumstances, to choose one's own way. [[03:10:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11428.4s)]
*  He meant that no matter what you're subjected to, no matter the pain, no matter the humiliation, the degradation that man or the devil himself could dream of inflicting, [[03:10:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11440.4s)]
*  there is something at your core that is still in your possession that cannot be taken from you until your own will falters and you decide to give it up. [[03:10:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11453.4s)]
*  Well, at Pites prison in Romania in the late 40s and early 50s, the communists set up an experiment to prove that this was not true. [[03:11:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11464.4s)]
*  In order for the experiment to succeed, the subject's defenses would have to be stripped away completely, and anything in which he might take refuge would have to be taken away from him. [[03:11:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11474.4s)]
*  This is why in every country where the communists took power in the 20th century, the institutions of family and faith and nation, those three things, were consistently and savagely attacked. [[03:11:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11486.4s)]
*  As Varlam Shalamov, the Russian writer who survived 17 years in the Gulag at Kolyma, wrote, [[03:11:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11500.4s)]
*  I saw that the only group of people able to preserve a minimum of humanity in conditions of starvation and abuse were the religious believers, the sectarians, almost all of them, and most priests. [[03:11:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11507.4s)]
*  This wasn't because they were constitutionally better people, but because they had shelter. [[03:12:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11520.4s)]
*  They had something to stabilize their minds and spirits, something to hold onto as they were tossed about in a sea of chaos and suffering. [[03:12:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11525.4s)]
*  This is the key difference between the authoritarian and the totalitarian. [[03:12:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11535.4s)]
*  The authoritarian wants your compliance. [[03:12:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11540.4s)]
*  The totalitarian wants everything. [[03:12:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11543.4s)]
*  Like the judge in Blood Meridian saying he experiences the freedom of birds as an insult. [[03:12:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11546.4s)]
*  With the anti-communist opposition in Romania very quickly crushed, Moscow sent advisors to help oversee this experiment. [[03:12:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11552.4s)]
*  And for their lab rats, they chose activists from the Romanian student movement. [[03:12:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11562.4s)]
*  They chose activists from the Romanian student movement. [[03:12:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11568.4s)]
*  Because see, with virtually all of Romania's leadership class dead or imprisoned by this point, the task of the resistance fell to their children's generation. [[03:12:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11572.4s)]
*  And in Romania, as elsewhere, colleges and universities were centers of political activity for enthusiastic young people. [[03:13:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11581.4s)]
*  These students, mostly, most of the students were the sons of peasants or middle class households, and virtually all of them were very devout Christians. [[03:13:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11589.4s)]
*  To this day, Romania is one of the most religious countries in Europe, and Christianity has been a central part of Romanian identity since the people emerged from the original Roman and Dacian stock all those centuries ago. [[03:13:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11598.4s)]
*  The patriotism and piety of these student anti-communists made them widely popular among the Romanian population, and their example was an inspiration to all of those out there who were still holding on to a shred of resistance in their hearts. [[03:13:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11612.4s)]
*  This was reason enough for the students as a class to be specially targeted, but those individuals brought to Piteș Prison had been selected for another reason, an additional one. [[03:13:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11629.4s)]
*  The student subjects of this experiment were specifically selected for their deep commitment to Christianity, for their hardened discipline and their Romanian patriotism. [[03:14:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11640.4s)]
*  Seminarians and students of theology were actually preferred for the stated purpose of the experiment was to destroy and reorder the personality, such that the objects of one's love and one's hatred could be reversed. [[03:14:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11651.4s)]
*  So take the men who are the most devout, the most attached to their families and communities, the most patriotic Romanians, and cause them by a predictable process to hate their religion, and hate their families, and hate their country. [[03:14:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11667.4s)]
*  If you could accomplish that with these men, then less difficult alterations of less fanatical personalities shouldn't be a problem. [[03:14:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11685.4s)]
*  The means by which this goal was to be achieved were pain and degradation and terror applied under the careful observation of psychologists, doctors, and political officers, again including advisors sent from Moscow. [[03:14:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11695.4s)]
*  Most of these students were already in prison, had been for a while. They had experienced deprivation, torture, and other forms of abuse already without cracking. That was just a prerequisite for consideration as a subject. [[03:15:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11710.4s)]
*  Those who showed the most courage in their resistance to the usual methods were selected and sent to the Securitate prison at Pitești. [[03:15:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11724.4s)]
*  And Alexander Solzhenitsyn called what happened at this prison in the late 40s and early 50s, the most terrible act of barbarism in the contemporary world. [[03:15:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11733.4s)]
*  The author of a book on the subject came to an awareness of the Pitești experiment while it was still ongoing. [[03:15:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11747.4s)]
*  He was himself a political prisoner of the Romanian Communists, and he described how he first learned that something terrible, more terrible than the mass killing and brutal torture that were already typical of the Romanian Communist regime by this point, that something even more terrible was happening. [[03:15:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11755.4s)]
*  He wrote, quote, My first night in Cluj, I spent in a vain attempt to adjust to a cell six and a half feet long and two feet wide. [[03:16:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11773.4s)]
*  The second night I was taken out into a search room and there I found myself in the company of three other prisoners who had been brought from the prison of Gerla. [[03:16:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11782.4s)]
*  I knew them. Two were students from Bucharest. The third was a worker. [[03:16:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11790.4s)]
*  Although we had been tried separately, the two students had been engaged in activities connected with mine. [[03:16:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11795.4s)]
*  We were placed in an automobile and taken to the depot. At eleven that night we left for Bucharest on a fast express train guarded by two securitate officers and a guard sergeant. [[03:16:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11801.4s)]
*  Bound in pairs by handcuffs, we were kept in a compartment that was unlighted to prevent our being recognized by other travelers. [[03:16:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11811.4s)]
*  It was night. Now and then the moon shone through the car window lighting the faces of the three. [[03:16:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11818.4s)]
*  It was strange faces. I had passed through many prisons in Romania. [[03:17:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11824.4s)]
*  I had met thousands of prisoners, but never had my eyes rested on such faces. [[03:17:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11829.4s)]
*  Beneath the pallor common to all prisoners, their faces reflected an exceptional physical weakness. [[03:17:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11834.4s)]
*  And over the emaciated faces a shadow of terror, a fixed expression of terror which stemmed from some uncommon experience, gave all three a frightening appearance. [[03:17:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11840.4s)]
*  When late in the night the student who was handcuffed to me fell asleep from exhaustion and rested his head on my shoulder, I could no longer suppress a reaction to the fear that came over me. [[03:17:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11851.4s)]
*  I moved my shoulder to wake him up. His head, illuminated by the light of the moon, appeared to be that of the corpse of one who had died surprised by a horror so hideous that it had accompanied him into the world beyond. [[03:17:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11861.4s)]
*  In former times he had been a swimming champion and a man of courage. Speech among ourselves was strictly forbidden. [[03:17:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11875.4s)]
*  Every now and then our eyes met, and there I could read the same terror that was impressed on their faces, a terror akin to madness." [[03:18:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11882.4s)]
*  And so he and the other prisoners were soon separated, and his own suffering in prison soon pushed that memory out of his mind, but then later, a little bit later, he was reminded of that incident in the train. [[03:18:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11891.4s)]
*  Later on, in the summer of 1952, I came again into contact with individuals who reminded me of the puzzle I had partly forgotten. [[03:18:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11903.4s)]
*  Other prisoners, transferred from the forced labor camps on the Danube Black Sea Canal, brought news that increased my suspicions regarding an entire category of prisoners who had once been the most dedicated and the most faithful defenders of the nation's freedom, the student body. [[03:18:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11911.4s)]
*  Accusations were brought against them which to the unknowing observer seemed utterly revolting, and yet the men who told me could not be lying, for they were speaking from experience of what they themselves had suffered. [[03:18:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11927.4s)]
*  The re-educated students, they said, beat them, denounced them, were spies for the secret police, increased the work norms, and tortured any who could not meet them. [[03:18:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11939.4s)]
*  All of these were accusations of an enormous gravity. [[03:19:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11949.4s)]
*  I wanted to believe that because the majority of these men were simple and untutored that they erred, making generalizations on the basis of their own personal experience, for I had known the students and in a totally different light. [[03:19:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11953.4s)]
*  But further news, instead of refuting what I hoped was not true, actually confirmed aspects which entered the domain of the tragic. [[03:19:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11965.4s)]
*  This time it was a student who spoke to me. [[03:19:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11973.4s)]
*  I had known him for years at the Polytechnical School in Bucharest. [[03:19:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11976.4s)]
*  At first he would not speak, he was afraid of everyone. [[03:19:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11980.4s)]
*  But when I told him I came to Constantin from Ayud, where, up to a few months previously, nothing out of the ordinary had happened, he loosened his tongue. [[03:19:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11983.4s)]
*  It was from him that I found out for the first time about the unmaskings. [[03:19:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11992.4s)]
*  The student warned me to fear the other students, and even to fear himself. [[03:19:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=11997.4s)]
*  Beware of the students as you would of Satan in person, even if they come under a mask of friendship, for they are perfidious. [[03:20:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12004.4s)]
*  They have done a lot of evil and some continue in their wrongdoing. [[03:20:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12011.4s)]
*  Why is it that everybody talks thus about the students? [[03:20:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12015.4s)]
*  What happened to them that they became so depraved? [[03:20:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12019.4s)]
*  For you know well that they were not like this before. [[03:20:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12022.4s)]
*  I do not know and I do not want to know what happened to them. [[03:20:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12025.4s)]
*  I am telling you only that they bite badly and on the sly. [[03:20:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12028.4s)]
*  Beware! [[03:20:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12031.4s)]
*  We did not know at that time, and perhaps he is still ignorant to the fact today, that in the process of degradation their souls were killed and they had passed through hell. [[03:20:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12033.4s)]
*  End quote. [[03:20:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12044.4s)]
*  And so it went like this. [[03:20:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12046.4s)]
*  As a preliminary to the process of unmasking, the students were put through the usual regime of abuse, sleep deprivation, starvation, and communist indoctrination. [[03:20:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12049.4s)]
*  Being committed political activists, the students were not expected to succumb to these, but the purpose of this initial stage was only to test the students' resolve in order to verify that they were fit subjects for the experiment to come. [[03:21:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12062.4s)]
*  Those who showed any signs of cracking in this initial stage were spared what was to come, and they were screened out. [[03:21:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12076.4s)]
*  They were instead sentenced to the usual terms of hard labor and indoctrination or were simply shot. [[03:21:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12083.4s)]
*  Only those students who scorned the communist crude attempts at reeducation were selected for reeducation at Pitesh. [[03:21:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12089.4s)]
*  When those selected arrived to Pitesh, they were confined, alone in the dark for a period of days or weeks, after which they were transferred to a cell that they shared with another inmate. [[03:21:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12097.4s)]
*  This other inmate would be another student, one who had already been through the Pitesh program or some portion of it and was now working with the prison authorities. [[03:21:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12109.4s)]
*  For the initial group, this role was played by a group of communist inmates who volunteered for it. [[03:21:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12118.4s)]
*  So their new cellmate had the job of befriending the new arrival and gaining his trust, and he would be left in that cell with him as long as it took for him to gather and report any and all information that might be useful to the authorities during what was to come. [[03:22:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12125.4s)]
*  Whenever possible, the new arrivals were placed with friends that they had known before and trusted before their arrest. [[03:22:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12141.4s)]
*  Students arrived in groups to Pitesh, and at a certain point, the group, along with their assigned cellmates, were led into a room and stood up in ranks. [[03:22:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12149.4s)]
*  A communist inmate, flanked by several others, would stand in front of the group and give a speech calling on them to denounce their old ways and embrace communism. [[03:22:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12160.4s)]
*  They'd heard all this before. The speech was so pat and corny that the confused students believed the guy was joking, doing some kind of a parody of communist propaganda, and so they began to joke back. [[03:22:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12170.4s)]
*  As soon as that happened, the speaker lifted his cap, and the communist inmates in front, as well as all of the cellmates who had spent weeks befriending the new arrivals, grabbed clubs which had been hidden beforehand and attacked. [[03:23:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12182.4s)]
*  Quote, With indescribable fury they began to hit him, with fists, cudgels, and feet, and to toss him from one to another until the bloodied wretch fell almost senseless and could no longer rise. [[03:23:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12196.4s)]
*  After they had given him a few more kicks to the head, two of them picked him up and threw him on the bunk, making him sit with his hands in his pockets and his head bowed according to the order. [[03:23:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12208.4s)]
*  Then another followed, then another, as though in a devilish ring dance intended to annihilate the last speck of physical and moral resistance of those who entered their rabid game. [[03:23:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12217.4s)]
*  End quote. The first-hand account of this first attack comes from one of the earliest pitesched inmates' subjects. [[03:23:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12227.4s)]
*  There followed a terrible scene, lasting unbelievably for several hours, during which one could hear only the thwacks of the bludgeons, the groans of the sufferers, and the profanity of the warden and his henchmen. [[03:23:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12234.4s)]
*  The student communists helped the guards every now and then, when some unfortunate managed to separate himself from the group of those beaten, and tried, futilely, to find a hiding place. [[03:24:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12246.4s)]
*  The guards dealt their blows with all the viciousness they could muster, venting their spite on us for having defied them previously. [[03:24:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12257.4s)]
*  Weakened by our designably inadequate diet, overwhelmed by the number and force of the guards as well as by the authority they represented, little by little we ceased our futile but still instinctive efforts to avoid the blows. [[03:24:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12264.4s)]
*  By now the guards struck us as they would so many empty sacks. The floor was full of urine and blood. [[03:24:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12276.4s)]
*  Prostrate and exhausted by beating, our bodies were strewn on the floor like corpses on a battlefield. Finally, the guards left the room. [[03:24:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12282.4s)]
*  We thought that it was finished. But this was only the beginning. For now, another group took over and set upon us. End quote. [[03:24:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12290.4s)]
*  And that was how the experiment began. [[03:24:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12299.4s)]
*  Severe beatings with clubs and whips and other things, randomly but consistently administered, were just background noise at pitesched. [[03:25:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12303.4s)]
*  Prisoners were beaten, often for hours at a time, as frequently as possible without killing them in order to keep them in a compromised state of suffering. [[03:25:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12311.4s)]
*  Doctors were kept on hand to ensure that the prisoners didn't die under torture and to revive them if they fainted or were knocked unconscious so that the torture could continue. [[03:25:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12321.4s)]
*  But otherwise the inmates were denied basic medical care, and so sores festered and skin rotted away because they were always filthy and forced to live in clothes soaked with blood, excrement and other bodily fluids. [[03:25:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12332.4s)]
*  They were kept on a starvation diet, of course, and denied regular sleep. Bright lights would be kept on during their sleep hours and inmates were required to sleep in a specific position without moving a muscle. [[03:25:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12345.4s)]
*  And another inmate, who was further ahead in his re-education, was assigned to stand over the sleeper with a club, and if the sleeper so much as twitched, the club was brought down as hard as possible, usually on the shins or the soles of the feet. [[03:25:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12358.4s)]
*  After a few times of being awakened by a hard club to the shins, inmates were so afraid of inadvertently moving while asleep that they rarely slept at all, and so over time became more and more disoriented and exhausted. [[03:26:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12373.4s)]
*  In the earlier discussion of the Forrest Brothers, I quoted Stalin's Approval of Torture. He said that the use of torture was absolutely correct and useful because it brought results and greatly accelerated the unmasking of enemies of the people. [[03:26:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12388.4s)]
*  That term, unmasking, seems straightforward enough. You're trying to hide something that the torturer unconceals, but unmasking was a technical term in communist torture regimes. [[03:26:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12402.4s)]
*  Dr. Shirley Spitz, in a paper called The Psychology of Torture, written in 1989, wrote, [[03:26:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12414.4s)]
*  Here we can mention the widely documented defense of identification with the aggressor. The torturer is introjected or swallowed whole as a psychic attempt to control an intolerable conflict situation. However, the victim also introjects the torturer's abusive and negative view of himself. [[03:27:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12445.4s)]
*  This can often lead to self-destructive attitudes and behaviors. Under conditions of torture, where emotions and physical reactions have to be repressed, the victim's sense of coherence and self-experience are shaken, and he begins to lose a sense of familiarity with himself. [[03:27:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12463.4s)]
*  His identity begins to fragment. If we add at this point the experience of extreme physical pain, where the contents of consciousness dissolve, he will experience a breakdown in his conviction about the very existence and reality of his external world and of his own reality of himself. [[03:27:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12479.4s)]
*  All that may be left is physical pain and the internalized definition of himself as non-human, worthless, and deserving of his torture. These unconscious, traumatic meanings that he attaches to his experience reflect the underlying shattering of archaic narcissistic fantasies. He can no longer believe in his own invulnerability, nor in the safety of a benign other." [[03:28:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12498.4s)]
*  The CIA's 1983 Human Resources Exploitation Training Manual puts it this way. [[03:28:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12522.4s)]
*  The purpose of all coercive techniques is to induce psychological regression in the subject by bringing a superior outside force to bear on his will to resist. Regression is basically a loss of autonomy, a reversion to an earlier behavioral level. [[03:28:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12530.4s)]
*  As the subject regresses, his learned personality traits fall away in a reverse chronological order. He begins to lose the capacity to carry out the highest creative activities, to deal with complex situations, to cope with stressful interpersonal relationships, or to cope with repeated frustrations." [[03:29:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12548.4s)]
*  It's worth mentioning that torture at Pitești was not intended to extract information. Again, unlike in some other Eastern Bloc countries, there was no civil war in Romania. There was no militant anti-communist resistance. The Red Army had taken care of that. [[03:29:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12568.4s)]
*  This was about something else. These inmates had mostly been incarcerated for some time, many of them years, and so any information they might have had would have been long obsolete. This wasn't about information. [[03:29:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12590.4s)]
*  Instead, the torturers would extract confessions of shameful events in the victim's life just to humiliate them, or force them to admit false confessions that they had knowledge of terrible crimes committed by their parents or priests or friends. [[03:30:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12604.4s)]
*  Torture at Pitești had one aim, to harm and to degrade and dehumanize in order to confuse and weaken the subject for the next stage of the experiment, called unmasking. [[03:30:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12618.4s)]
*  Or as the writer Baku puts it in The Anti-Humans, a book about the Pitești prison, [[03:30:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12632.4s)]
*  Investigations conducted in the Ministry of the Interior and in various regional securitates managed to wrest quite a few secrets from the students, not so much because of moral weakness as by means of brutal methods of interrogation. [[03:30:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12638.4s)]
*  These were such that it was almost impossible for a student to deny an offense even if he had committed none. He admitted the crime to avoid further torture. [[03:30:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12652.4s)]
*  But even though the securitate did succeed in tearing secrets from tortured minds, it was unable to affect the structure of the soul. [[03:31:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12661.4s)]
*  On the contrary, having passed through these investigations, the students came out more convinced than ever of the righteousness of the cause for which they were suffering, and of the absurdity of the newly imposed system. [[03:31:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12669.4s)]
*  As long then as the soul remained unaltered, there had been no defeat. So it was precisely the soul that remained the principal target, its utter destruction, the aim. [[03:31:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12680.4s)]
*  Those who masterminded and directed the operation wanted more than the mere torturing of the victims. [[03:31:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12691.4s)]
*  They were determined to penetrate into the most intimate recesses of the human soul, probing and prodding it, finding even the smallest cleavages, [[03:31:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12697.4s)]
*  discovering everything that can be struck, broken, destroyed in man to leave him only a body made passive and void of volition. [[03:31:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12706.4s)]
*  Beasts kill out of biological necessity, to feed. But the beast-man, when he uses reason to implement his hatred, knows no limits. [[03:31:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12714.4s)]
*  Only men capable of both great lucidity and frenzied hate could have decreed piteshed. [[03:32:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12723.4s)]
*  From another book on this, called The Devil's Mill by Eugen Magarescu, we have this. [[03:32:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12731.4s)]
*  In a so-called act of depersonalization, students were forced under torture, permanent and unimaginable torture, to betray all that they held dear, God, their own parents, brothers, sisters, friends. [[03:32:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12739.4s)]
*  They were constrained to drink urine and eat feces. The human being was thereby annihilated. Disgusted at his weakness, he would never be able to recover himself before his own conscience. [[03:32:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12754.4s)]
*  The pain was beyond human endurance. Then they undressed me. What followed is indescribable. [[03:32:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12764.4s)]
*  Beatings on the head to induce stupefaction, beatings on the face for disfigurement, thousands of blows to the back below the ribs, to the solar plexus and to the soles of my feet. [[03:32:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12770.4s)]
*  Dozens of fainting, dozens of times fainting, and then all over again, for hours and hours on end. They shattered my ribs, my lungs, my liver, kicking my bones, my kidneys with shod feet. [[03:33:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12781.4s)]
*  End quote. [[03:33:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12794.4s)]
*  One of the communist primary weapons was time. They had all the time in the world. [[03:33:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12796.4s)]
*  An inmate who was still holding on to something, anything that made him human. [[03:33:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12803.4s)]
*  And something other than clay in the experimenter's hands could be told that, look, countless others have already been through this program. [[03:33:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12809.4s)]
*  People way stronger than you. They all felt just like you thought. And 100% of them had been broken completely. [[03:33:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12817.4s)]
*  And these young men were not tortured for days or weeks, but every day in shifts without reprieve for months. [[03:33:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12826.4s)]
*  They were told that it would go on as long as it had to, that they would be tortured and tortured. [[03:33:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12836.4s)]
*  And if they passed out, the torture would continue when they woke up. [[03:34:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12843.4s)]
*  And they weren't trapped in a cave by ISIS. There was no hope, however dim, of Delta Force coming to the rescue. The communists were in control. [[03:34:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12849.4s)]
*  You couldn't hope that the authorities would find out what was happening. The authorities were doing it. [[03:34:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12860.4s)]
*  The torturer could threaten that even if the victim went into a coma for 30 years, that he'd be there waiting in the hospital room when he woke up. [[03:34:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12866.4s)]
*  It's a different thing to be tortured and not merely beaten or mutilated, but tortured in a way designed by people who sat down around a table and figured out ways meant to drive your pain to the highest possible intensity. [[03:34:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12875.4s)]
*  And to know that there is no hope coming from the outside. [[03:34:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12889.4s)]
*  As doctrinaire atheists and materialists, a central claim of the communists in the 20th century was that the material world is all there is. [[03:34:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12894.4s)]
*  And so history and politics and human psychology are all subject to the same natural forces that govern falling bodies and chemical reactions. [[03:35:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12903.4s)]
*  The experiment at Pitesh took this claim to its logical conclusion with regard to the individual person. [[03:35:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12913.4s)]
*  Its purpose was to demonstrate, its ostensible purpose was to demonstrate that there was no soul. [[03:35:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12920.4s)]
*  There was no hidden kernel, no mystery at the heart of man that could not be cut out and laid on the operating table for scientific prodding. [[03:35:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12927.4s)]
*  Your beliefs, your values, your loves, your loyalties are just ephemera. [[03:35:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12938.4s)]
*  Those are masks worn over the true man, which in his essence is no different from any other animal. [[03:35:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12943.4s)]
*  And for this reason, the experiment is referred to the crucial stages of their program as unmasking. [[03:35:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12950.4s)]
*  Once subjects had been reduced to the condition of animals, they could be shaped without interference by the principles of operant conditioning. [[03:35:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12957.4s)]
*  Just as was Pavlov's dog and B.F. Skinner's animal subjects or Alex from A Clockwork Orange. [[03:36:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12966.4s)]
*  But first they had to be pulled down to that level. [[03:36:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12974.4s)]
*  And so inmates were required to eat like animals, on all fours without using their hands. [[03:36:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12978.4s)]
*  They were made to empty their bowels and their bladders in the same dish in which their food was served and they were forbidden from washing it. [[03:36:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12984.4s)]
*  They were required to clean filthy toilets with their mouths. [[03:36:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12991.4s)]
*  When they vomited, they were required to eat the vomit and everything it contained. [[03:36:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=12995.4s)]
*  This is from an account taken by Kostin Mariska in the Pitesh tragedy. [[03:36:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13001.4s)]
*  Quote, You were made to pull at each other's genitals, or one of them would put his penis in your mouth. [[03:36:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13006.4s)]
*  If you soiled yourself during beatings, you were made to eat your own feces and to lick the dirty long johns, [[03:36:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13012.4s)]
*  or to eat another's feces from your own mess tin without being allowed to wash it after that. [[03:36:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13018.4s)]
*  You were made to kiss each other's bottoms. You were made to urinate in each other's mouths. [[03:37:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13023.4s)]
*  When you begged for water, you would be given urine from the bucket, or they would urinate in your mouth, or others would spit in your mouth. [[03:37:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13028.4s)]
*  You were made to spit in each other's bottoms and then lick it up. They would wipe a stick smeared in feces on your mouth and in your mouth. [[03:37:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13035.4s)]
*  You were made to stick your finger up your bottom and then suck it. End quote. [[03:37:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13042.4s)]
*  Typically, once the program had been going on for a while, these tortures would be administered by other prisoners, other student prisoners under coercion. [[03:37:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13048.4s)]
*  The designers of the experiment had created a kind of evil genius, [[03:37:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13057.4s)]
*  self-reinforcing system of escalating torture by involving the inmates in this way. [[03:37:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13063.4s)]
*  Because one of the recurring questions that would be posed to inmates under torture [[03:37:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13068.4s)]
*  was whether any of their fellow inmates that were assigned as their persecutors had shown any signs of leniency toward them, any sympathy toward them. [[03:37:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13073.4s)]
*  Had anyone held back with the club? Had anyone ever shown you mercy during a beating? [[03:38:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13082.4s)]
*  Had you ever moved while sleeping and the person who was supposed to hit you with the club let you off the hook? [[03:38:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13088.4s)]
*  Had anyone ever shared food with you? Had anybody helped you in any way? [[03:38:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13095.4s)]
*  Had anyone shown any compassion? [[03:38:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13100.4s)]
*  The inmate torturers, they were further ahead in the program. They'd all been through this themselves already. [[03:38:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13103.4s)]
*  And so they knew from their own experience that no one would stand up to the torture over time. [[03:38:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13110.4s)]
*  So when it was their turn to be the torturer, they removed all the brakes on their cruelty for fear that they would then later be accused of holding back [[03:38:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13115.4s)]
*  and find themselves cycled back to the beginning of the program, which is what would happen. [[03:38:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13124.4s)]
*  And most of them were cycled back through several times anyway for real or invented reasons just to remove any impression they had some kind of control over their circumstances. [[03:38:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13128.4s)]
*  Yet even still, torturing your best friends, because that's what these were, the hardcore student movement was a small and closely knit group. [[03:38:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13137.4s)]
*  And many of them not only knew each other, but they'd been through a lot together. [[03:39:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13150.4s)]
*  Torturing your comrades and being tortured by them, this was still just condition setting. [[03:39:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13155.4s)]
*  Preparation for the true purpose of the experiment, which again was to reorder the personality. [[03:39:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13161.4s)]
*  The most fundamental values and beliefs of these men, who have been preselected for their rigid discipline, their patriotism and their commitment to Christianity. [[03:39:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13169.4s)]
*  Performances on religious subjects, such as black masses staged at Easter or Christmas, horrified the detainees. [[03:39:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13179.4s)]
*  On such occasions, it was the theology students who were to suffer the most, dressed up as Christ's, clothed in cassocks and smeared with excrement. [[03:39:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13187.4s)]
*  They were made to take communion with urine and feces standing in for bread and wine. [[03:39:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13195.4s)]
*  And instead of the cross, a phallus was fashioned, which all the others were made to kiss. [[03:40:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13200.4s)]
*  Alongside them, hymns were sung with evil words in which the common places were insults against Christ and the Virgin Mary. [[03:40:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13205.4s)]
*  Sometimes the detainees would be stripped naked and sexual plays were performed on the orders of the guards. [[03:40:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13212.4s)]
*  On Good Friday, he assigned inmates their roles. [[03:40:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13218.4s)]
*  This one is Joseph, another is Mary Magdalene, the Virgin, Christ and so forth. [[03:40:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13222.4s)]
*  As well as one assigned to play a donkey. [[03:40:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13227.4s)]
*  And they were forced to perform. [[03:40:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13230.4s)]
*  The donkey is philated by Mary Magdalene and then sodomized by Joseph before ending with its muzzle between the legs of the Virgin Mary while being sodomized by Jesus. [[03:40:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13233.4s)]
*  The guards displayed a diabolical pleasure in mocking the faithful. [[03:40:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13242.4s)]
*  Such scenes had a terrible effect on the victims who, as a rule, had found their only solace in the faith itself. [[03:40:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13247.4s)]
*  However, after participating in these black masses, their entire faith was shaken to its foundations. [[03:40:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13253.4s)]
*  One favorite tactic of the guards was to chant baptismal rites while buckets of urine and feces were brought before the inmates whose heads would be pushed down into the sewage until it filled their lungs and they began to drown from it. [[03:41:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13262.4s)]
*  The head was pulled out long enough for the inmate to take a breath and regain his senses enough to hear the religious chanting before he was re-submerged again and again and again in a mockery of the baptismal rite. [[03:41:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13274.4s)]
*  When they vomited excrement, they were beaten and forced to eat it. [[03:41:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13287.4s)]
*  A prisoner would be smeared in excrement and dressed in the phony vestments of a priest while others were forced to come before him, kneel, cross themselves, and intone a reverential prayer and then lick feces from his genitals or his behind. [[03:41:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13291.4s)]
*  Prisoners would be forced to perform sex acts on one another or they would be sodomized with large clubs and other painful instruments while being held down face to face with an icon of Christ or the Virgin Mary while liturgical music played. [[03:41:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13306.4s)]
*  The goal of that was simple. [[03:42:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13322.4s)]
*  It was apparent to anyone who had seen a clockwork orange it was to cause the inmates on a deep unconscious level to associate the symbols of their Christian faith with suffering and degradation. [[03:42:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13324.4s)]
*  Each of these prisoners, by definition, had been willing to risk his life by engaging in anti-communist activism and every one of them would have rather died than torture their friends or endure the torments of this prison. [[03:42:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13336.4s)]
*  And so the authorities took great care to prevent any possibility of suicide because the prisoners would take the narrowest opportunity for it. [[03:42:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13351.4s)]
*  In one instance, a prisoner was being led up to a cell on a third floor mezzanine and when his guard got temporarily distracted just for one moment, in that one moment of distraction, he took the opportunity and threw himself to the concrete floor below and died. [[03:42:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13361.4s)]
*  All sharp objects would have to be kept from them because there would be no hesitation if they had the opportunity to take it and go for one of their vital arteries. [[03:42:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13376.4s)]
*  Several members of one class, for lack of a better word, tore out the veins in their wrists using their teeth and so the others in the class had their teeth knocked out. [[03:43:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13386.4s)]
*  After that, other measures were put in place to make sure that inmates were under supervision and control at all times to prevent suicide. [[03:43:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13396.4s)]
*  Quote, everything of the past which could offer any kind of refuge was to be muddied and denigrated. [[03:43:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13404.4s)]
*  This included the heroes of history and the folklore of Christian inspiration. [[03:43:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13410.4s)]
*  Then to be given special attention was the destruction of love for family in order to completely isolate the victim in his own misery, bereft of religion, love of country and family. [[03:43:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13414.4s)]
*  This would break the chain that links together a community of national thought and gives meaning to a national struggle. [[03:43:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13425.4s)]
*  When the individual was thus cut off from his history, faith and family, the ultimate step in reeducating him was to destroy his existence as a personality, as an individual. [[03:43:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13432.4s)]
*  This, to the victim, was to prove the most painful step of all and was called his unmasking. [[03:44:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13442.4s)]
*  The torture continued during the unmasking stage because, again, the torture was mostly just condition setting. [[03:44:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13450.4s)]
*  That was just their, again, background noise, just to keep them in the proper state of openness and vulnerability and dependency. [[03:44:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13457.4s)]
*  During inmates unmasking, when they were being reprogrammed, they would be made to do things like write sworn affidavits, accusing their families and friends and priests of all manner of barbaric behavior. [[03:44:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13466.4s)]
*  You know, mothers prostituting themselves to priests, fathers raping their daughters and so on. [[03:44:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13480.4s)]
*  And those letters would be signed and then brought back to the inmates' home villages and circulated around the community, shown to their parents, shown to their neighbors. [[03:44:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13486.4s)]
*  It's worth emphasizing again that none of this was meant to extract information. [[03:44:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13499.4s)]
*  It's also worth mentioning that even calling it an experiment, I think, it rings pretty false. [[03:45:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13505.4s)]
*  Even taking the clockwork orange aspect at face value, the means were so crude and haphazard that it's very hard to avoid the conclusion that the experiment was just an official euphemism for putting these men through hell just because they could. [[03:45:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13511.4s)]
*  These educated, nationalist, deeply Christian young men were the flower of the Romanian nation. [[03:45:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13530.4s)]
*  They had been the bulwark against communism before the Red Army arrived. [[03:45:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13536.4s)]
*  And now they were in the hands of their enemies, again, the majority of whom at this stage were not even ethnic Romanians. [[03:45:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13541.4s)]
*  And for all the scientific gloss on these events, the accounts are hardly different in any detail from what you'd expect to read about people who had fallen into the hands of a deranged serial killer. [[03:45:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13547.4s)]
*  A further piece of evidence that the whole idea of an experiment was only a fig leaf is the fact that after the experiment at Piteș, most of the students were sent to slave labor camps and worked to death anyway. [[03:45:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13558.4s)]
*  So it's not as if the authorities were real concerned with whether their personalities had been truly sustainably altered. [[03:46:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13571.4s)]
*  I'm sure if I thought about it for a while, I could think of a clever way to end this episode. [[03:46:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13578.4s)]
*  But to be honest, I just wanted to end. And I'm sure you do as well. [[03:46:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13583.4s)]
*  I think what made me decide to do this travesty of a podcast episode in the first place was Jaco and I talking about Joe McCarthy and the Red Scarecrow. [[03:46:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13588.4s)]
*  The early fifties in one of our unraveling episodes and thinking as I was going through a lot of the material and commentary on that period that, you know, yeah, there was a lot of demagoguery and excesses during the Red Scarecrow, but also to being struck by the fact that too many people just have no understanding of what we were really dealing with here. [[03:46:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13601.4s)]
*  It had never been anything like the Soviet Union under Stalin, not at that scale and with that kind of power and with those global totalizing ambitions. [[03:46:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13618.4s)]
*  And the funny thing is, as instinctually conservative as I am in certain ways, I am not the only one who is going to be in the red scare. [[03:47:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13628.4s)]
*  But the version of Marxism refracted through Lenin and politically manifested in the USSR that sought not only to smash capitalism and replace it with centrally planned collectivist economics, but made it its main focus. [[03:47:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13638.4s)]
*  But the version of Marxism refracted through Lenin and politically manifested in the USSR that sought not only to smash capitalism and replace it with centrally planned collectivist economics, but made it its mission to destroy everything that people had valued for thousands of years. [[03:47:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13653.4s)]
*  To cause children to hate their parents and parents to suspect their children, to make people hate their national culture and disavow their faith and spit on their heritage and their traditions. [[03:47:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OlJfplzkkM4&t=13675.4s)]
